#!/usr/bin/env python3
import requests
from requests.auth import HTTPBasicAuth

account_sid = "AC39ed37a2d9e427ea7aeb4c27aa368110"
auth_token = "3590e08c47cfbb31093592ec84ab4af0"
from_number = "+15615324683"
to_number = "+13057768712"

# Point to a TwiML URL that will connect back to our bot via AudioSocket
twiml_url = "http://demo.twilio.com/docs/voice.xml"  # Test TwiML first

url = f"https://api.twilio.com/2010-04-01/Accounts/{account_sid}/Calls.json"

data = {
    "From": from_number,
    "To": to_number,
    "Url": twiml_url
}

response = requests.post(url, data=data, auth=HTTPBasicAuth(account_sid, auth_token))
print(f"Status: {response.status_code}")
if response.status_code == 201:
    print("✅ Call initiated successfully via Twilio REST API")
    print(f"Call SID: {response.json()['sid']}")
else:
    print(f"❌ Error: {response.text}")
EOF
